<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Interim Management Report<a name="InterimManagementReport_043238"></a></font></b></h1>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. Business Activity</font></b><a name="a1_BusinessActivity_043240"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
(&#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148; or &#147;the Company&#148;) is a leading provider of deposition
equipment to the semiconductor industry. The Company&#146;s technology solutions are
used by a diverse range of customers worldwide to build advanced components for
electronic and opto-electronic applications based on compound, silicon, or
organic semiconductor materials. Such components are used in displays,
signaling, lighting, fiber optic communication systems, wireless and mobile
telephony applications, optical and electronic storage devices, computing, as
well as a range of other leading-edge technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company markets and sells its products worldwide, principally through its
direct sales organization and appointed dealers and sales representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
business activities include developing, producing and installing equipment for
coating semiconductor materials, process engineering, consulting and training,
including ongoing customer support.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
supplies to customers both full production-scale chemical vapor deposition
systems and small scale systems for Research and Development use and
small-scale production use.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
product range includes customized production and research scale compound
semiconductor systems capable of depositing material films on up to 95 x
two-inch diameter wafers per single production run, or smaller multiples of 4
to 6 inch diameter wafers, employing Metal-Organic Chemical Vapor Deposition (&#147;MOCVD&#148;)
or organic thin film deposition on up to Gen. 3.5 substrates, including Polymer
Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;PVPD&#148;) or Organic Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148;) for Organic
Light Emitting Diodes (&#147;OLED&#148;) applications or Plasma Enhanced Chemical Vapor
Phase Deposition (&#147;PECVD&#148;) for depositing complex Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon
Nanotubes or Nanowires). AIXTRON also manufactures full production and research
scale deposition systems for silicon semiconductor market applications capable
of depositing material films on wafers of up to 300 mm diameter, employing
technologies such as: Chemical Vapor Deposition (&#147;CVD&#148;), Atomic Vapor
Deposition (&#147;AVD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148;) and Atomic Layer Deposition (&#147;ALD&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\105621\09-19734-1\task3647439\19734-1-bi.htm',USER='105621',CD='Jul 29 19:33 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. Important Factors of the Reporting Period</font></b><a name="a2_ImportantFactorsOfTheReporting_043253"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TV
backlighting driving increased order demand</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Rising demand for LED
applications and TV backlighting in particular, has resulted in 85% higher
order intake in Q2/2009 of EUR 57.9m over Q1/2009 (EUR 31.2m), bringing to an
end a five quarter run of declining demand. The outlook for the second half of 2009
remains positive with forward visibility back to two quarters.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenues have increased by 23%
over the previous quarter to reach EUR 56.7m in Q2/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Capacity
expansions of LED manufacturers</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the previous live
quarters, market nervousness and customer inventory reduction programs,
triggered by the financial crisis and recession, had led to progressively low
and erratic utilization rates at many customers&#146; production facilities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This situation changed in Q2.
Reasons for the rapid reversal in Q2 were improving LED market conditions and
growing customer confidence, fuelled by a more positive outlook and the
increased speed of adoption of LEDs in backlighting and other applications,
including some early street light modules. This market improvement led to many
LED producers reporting 100% utilization rates by the end of Q2/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Multiple
and scheduled orders return</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Unlike Q1/2009, where the
majority of orders received were for small sub-five volume orders, in Q2 we
received an increased number of multiple and scheduled orders which could
potentially indicate the beginning of a period of market recovery.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On May&nbsp;25, 2009, for
example, AIXTRON announced a purchase contract with Chinese Hualei
Optoelectronic Ltd. for multiple MOCVD systems, which will be used for the
production of high brightness LEDs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;2, 2009, AIXTRON
announced a further multiple system order from Epistar, Taiwan &#151; recorded as
order intake in H1/2009. This MOCVD system order was placed to increase the
production capacity for high brightness LEDs at Epistar.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Penetration
of LED backlighting technology in TVs gaining momentum</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With the increasing public and
government interest in &#147;green technology&#148;, most leading TV manufacturers are
developing LED-backlit LCD TVs in 2009. The benefits of improved picture
quality, the thinner form factor and the power saving advantages of LED
technology are being heavily promoted in the marketing of these new products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">According to iSuppli, the
shipments of LCD TV panels with LED backlighting are expected to rise 200 fold
to 90 million units in 2013, up from just 438,000 LED TV panels in 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While Samsung Electronics has
clearly established a strong early position in the &#147;LED TV&#148; market by launching
a range of LED TVs in March, its competitors, including Sony and LG
Electronics, have been rapidly responding with new LED TV models of their own
in Q2/2009. The largest US retail volume LCD TV maker, VIZIO, has also recently
announced that its first LED TVs would be available in September.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increased competition for
market share of what is still a premium price market is already beginning to
show signs of price erosion as the volumes shipped increase. The largest global
volume shipper of LED backlit TVs, Samsung, has indicated that they intend to
have shipped more than 2 million LED TVs by the end of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With the reported
higher-than-expected demand for LED backlit LCD TVs, and the increase in
manufacturers trying to source high Brightness LEDs, the demand for AIXTRON LED
manufacturing equipment has gathered momentum during Q2 and looks set to
continue into the second half of the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">US-Dollar
drifting lower against the Euro</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After the period of strength
for the US-Dollar against the Euro seen at the beginning of the year, the US-currency
drifted lower against the Euro starting in March, eventually breaching the USD
1.40 level by end of May. The returning appetite for risk in the global equity
markets has had the consequent effect of diminishing the perceived safe haven
status of the US-Dollar.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, reflecting the
fragile state of economic confidence, the US-Dollar again marginally gained
strength again towards the end of Q2, supported by a drop in risk appetite as
global equity and commodity markets traded lower. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nevertheless, the average USD/EUR
exchange rate of the second quarter of 2009 was USD 1.36, 15% stronger than the
USD 1.56 average of Q2/2008, which has in turn positively influenced AIXTRON&#146;s
Q2/2009 comparable revenues and EBIT as more than 70% of AIXTRON revenues in
H1/2009 were transacted in US-Dollars, but with only c. 20% of the company&#146;s
cost being in US-Dollars.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON routinely employs
hedging instruments to mitigate the effects of currency movements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">New
Carbon Nanotubes (CNT) Research Project</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During Q2/2009, the 3-year
EU-funded &#147;Technotubes&#148; research project was formally started. The project
consortium is composed of European R&amp;D institutions, AIXTRON as the
equipment partner, and end-user representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The project aims to develop,
the first automated equipment for mass production of carbon nanotubes on 300 mm
wafers with elements of the project consequently covering the design,
engineering, process development, control, and material qualification processes
also the team involved develop potential prototype applications which could
directly benefit from low cost, volume CNT production.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2007, AIXTRON acquired
Nanoinstruments, a UK-based business with, PECVD expertise in CNT deposition
technology which now also utilizes AIXTRON showerhead technology. The AIXTRON
Group has considerable development experience of showerhead technology,
evidenced by the significant market share of the Company&#146;s CRIUS</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;MOCVD equipment. The &#147;Technotubes&#148; project
will draw on this expertise in pursuit of the project&#146;s objectives.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of
Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.
Results of Operations</font></b><a name="a3_ResultsOfOperations_043418"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1. Development of
Revenues</font></b><a name="a3_1_DevelopmentOfRevenues_043420"></a></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the first half of 2009, AIXTRON recorded revenues of EUR&nbsp;102.9m, a
decrease of EUR&nbsp;25.3m, or 20%, compared to EUR&nbsp;128.2m in the same six
month period last year. Despite the beneficial effects of a stronger average
US-Dollar rate and the increasing revenue volume trend within the first six
months of the year, these recent positive development could not compensate positive
for weaker comparable Year-on-Year revenues.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
change in revenues Year-on-Year was largely driven by lower sales of compound
semiconductor deposition equipment, especially in the first quarter of 2009 (</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">H1/2009:
EUR 88.7m or 86% of total revenues; H1/2008: EUR 104.9m or 82%)</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">, being purchased
by customers predominantly for the production of LEDs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenues
from silicon semiconductor deposition equipment decreased to EUR 4.2m or 4% of
total revenues (H1/2008: EUR 10.0m or 8%). This is a direct consequence of the
continued depressed memory market conditions and consequently suppressed
capital spending by AIXTRON&#146;s customers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
in H1/2008, total equipment sales generated 90% of total revenues in H1/2009.
The remaining revenues were generated by sales of spare parts and service.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.82%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-3.3</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.84%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="9%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:9.18%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-25</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.66%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">75%
of total revenues in H1/2009 were delivered to customers in Asia. The
comparatively high European revenue share (19% in H1/2009 versus 5% in H1/2008)
was significantly influenced by the Plastic Logic revenue recorded in Q1/2009.
The remaining revenues, with a 6% share, were generated in the USA.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.8</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\JMS\rcheney\09-19734-1\task3647319\19734-1-bk.htm',USER='rcheney',CD='Jul 29 07:55 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cost of
sales</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> improved significantly from 61% of revenues to 57% of revenues. In absolute
terms, cost of sales reduced by 25% from EUR&nbsp;77.8m in H1/2008 to
EUR&nbsp;58.4m in H1/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Consequently,
the <b>gross margin</b> improved by 4 percentage
points from 39% of revenues to 43% of revenues. In absolute terms, the Company&#146;s
<b>gross profit</b> reduced by 12% to
EUR&nbsp;44.5m in H1/2009 (H1/2008: EUR&nbsp;50.3m). The improved gross margin
percentage resulted from a more favorable revenue mix with a higher percentage
of final acceptances especially in the first quarter of 2009 and a favorable
USD/EUR exchange rate.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared
to the first half of 2008, <b>operating costs</b>
in H1/2009 decreased by 2% to EUR 32.2m in absolute terms. At the same time,
operating costs relative to revenues in percentage terms increased from 25% in
H1/2008 to 30% in H1/2009, influenced by the following factors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Selling
expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> relative to revenues improved to 9% of revenues in
the first half of 2009 (H1/2008: 11%). In absolute terms, the <b>selling expenses</b> were by 35% lower at EUR&nbsp;9.5m
year-on-year (H1/2008: EUR 14.6m). This improvement in relative and absolute
terms was mainly due to regional mix and volume related variable sales
commissions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">General
and administration expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> remained relatively stable at
EUR 9.6m or 9% of revenues in H1/2009 (H1/2008: EUR&nbsp;9.2m or 7% of
revenues).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared
to the same period last year,<b> Research and development
spending</b> increased by EUR 2.8m or 20% in H1/2009 to EUR 16.9m
(H1/2008: EUR 14.1m), the largest single element being the expense for one
publicly funded R&amp;D project of EUR 1.6m in Q1/2009. Relative to revenues,
R&amp;D spending increased by 5 percentage points from 11% to 16%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
continued focus on </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">R&amp;D (for both Silicon
and Compound equipment) is driven by our determination to remain a major player
in markets judged by many to be significant growth opportunities for many years
to come.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Other
operating income and expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> was a net income of
EUR&nbsp;3.8m in the first half of 2009 which was 25% less than the figure in
the same period of 2008 (H1/2008: EUR&nbsp;5.1m of income).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Accounted for in the other operating income and
expenses of</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> H1/2009 are higher R&amp;D grants of EUR 1.7m (H1/2008: EUR 1.0m) and negative
foreign exchange effects (H1/2009: EUR -3.8m; H1/2008: EUR +3.4m) arising
principally from USD/EUR currency movements and hedging contract premiums
(H1/2009: EUR 1.8m; H1/2008 : nil).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Accounted
for in the other operating income and expenses of H1/2009 are higher R&amp;D
grants of EUR 1.7m (H1/2008: EUR 1.0m) and negative foreign exchange effects
principally from the USD/EUR-rate of EUR -3.8m (H1/2008: EUR +3.4m), including
hedging contract premiums of EUR 1.8m (H1/2008: nil).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also
included are the gains from the sale of the Aachen office building (EUR 1.3m)
and </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a compensation payment for a cancelled order (EUR
2.5m), both booked in Q1/2009. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Without those two items totalling
EUR&nbsp;3.8m, the H1/2009 net other operating income and expenses would have
resulted in a figure of EUR&nbsp;0.0m.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating
income (EBIT)</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <b>in H1/2009</b>  <b>was at</b> EUR&nbsp;12.3m with a 12% margin in H1/2009, 30%
lower year-on-year (H1/2008: EUR 17.6m; 14% margin), principally due to lower revenue,
lower gains from foreign exchange effects.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However,
when comparing the two H1/2009 sequential quarters, the Q2/2009 EBIT of
EUR&nbsp;4.7m (8% margin) was 24% higher than the &#147;recurring&#148; Q1/2009 EBIT of
EUR&nbsp;3.8m (8% margin) principally because of the volume effect and exactly
in line with previously published expectations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Result
before taxes</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> decreased 33% from EUR 19.1m in H1/2008 to EUR 12.7m
in H1/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
recorded a <b>tax expense</b> of EUR 3.9m of the
profit before tax in the first half of 2009, with an effective tax rate of 31%,
similar to H1/2008 (EUR 5.7m or 30% of the profit before </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">97</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">161.3</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">98</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-55.3</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-34</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">%</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s total first half 2009 <b>equipment
order intake</b> declined by 44% compared to the previous year&#146;s first
half, marking the peak and trough of the previous investment cycle</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">in the LED industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, comparing the two sequential quarters of
H1/2009, we saw an increasing order intake level from EUR 31.2m in Q1/2009 to
EUR 57.9m in Q2/2009, representing an 85% increase. This positive development
confirms our previous prediction that Q1/2009 would mark </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the low point in
the current investment cycle, with some very strong signals that the speed of
adoption of such applications such as LED backlighting has increased
significantly in the last 3 months and is likely to remain so for the remainder
of the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Order
intake for compound semiconductor equipment</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
continues to come from customers who are predominantly focused on the
production of high brightness LEDs and the corresponding end-market
applications, but </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">decreased by 41% to EUR 88.4m from EUR 149.6m in
H1/2008, representing 99% of the total value of equipment orders received by
AIXTRON in the first half of 2009 (95% in H1/2008).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
proportion of orders received for silicon semiconductor equipment dropped to 1%
of total equipment order intake, from 5% in H1/2008. In absolute numbers, the
order intake for silicon semiconductor equipment decreased by 93% to EUR 0.6m
in H1/2009 from EUR 8.4m in H1/2008, due to the persistently negative memory
market environment. Management believes that there is little evidence to
suggest that this situation will improve during the course of this year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Separately,
the development work being conducted on next-generation memory and logic
equipment continues, with customer demonstrations and film development work
being done within the company&#146;s research labs and at customers&#146; facilities.
This work, combined with the involvement of Sunnyvale staff in next generation
Compound and other group nano-technology projects, means that the team in
Sunnyvale continue to make a positive and valuable contribution to the group&#146;s
objectives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b>equipment order backlog</b>
of EUR 109.4m at June&nbsp;30, 2009 is 34% lower than at the same point in time
in 2008 (EUR 165.1m) which represented the peak of orders of the previous
investment cycle. Sequentially, the equipment order backlog improved from EUR
100.7m as of March&nbsp;31, 2009 to EUR 109.4m. The Management expects that
about EUR 100m of that backlog will be converted into revenues by the end of
the year 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The order backlog for compound semiconductor equipment
was EUR 106.0m as of June&nbsp;30, 2009 (97% of total backlog), representing a
34% decrease year-on-year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The remaining backlog figure of EUR </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.3m (3% of total
backlog) is made up of silicon semiconductor equipment orders convertible into
revenues in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
a matter of internal policy, AIXTRON records only equipment orders as actual
order intake and order backlog, if the Company has received a firm purchase
order, an agreed deposit and a customer-confirmed delivery date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Financial Position</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;"> and
Net Assets</font><a name="a4_FinancialPositionAndNetAssets_043437"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company recorded no <b>bank borrowings</b> as of June&nbsp;30, 2009
and December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
<b>equity ratio</b> increased to 74% as of June&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2009,
from 68% as of December&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2008, principally due to higher retained
earnings, the dividend payment, lower inventories and a consequently lower
balance sheet total.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The AIXTRON Group&#146;s <b>capital
expenditures</b> of the first half of 2009 amounted to EUR 4.0m
(H1/2008: EUR 5.7m), the large majority of which was related to purchases of
technical equipment (including testing and laboratory equipment).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>property, plant and equipment</b> decreased to
EUR&nbsp;32.8m as per June&nbsp;30,
2009 (</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 39.3m as of December&nbsp;31,
2008), principally due to the sale of the Aachen office building and the higher
of depreciation compared to capital expenditures, mostly in technical equipment</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in recorded <b>goodwill </b>from
</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 58.7m as per December&nbsp;31, 2008 t</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o
EUR</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> 59.1m as
per June&nbsp;30, 2009 resulted purely from currency translation. There were no
additions or impairments in the first half of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>other intangible assets</b>
decreased </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">from EUR 10.3m as per December&nbsp;31, 2008 to</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> EUR 8.8m as per June&nbsp;30,
2009 principally due to depreciation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and
cash equivalents including cash deposits</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased by 20% to
EUR&nbsp;84.4m (EUR 74.4m + EUR 10.0m) as of June&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2009 compared
to EUR&nbsp;70.5m (EUR 67.5m + EUR 3.0m) as of December&nbsp;31, 2008. The
period end cash position is after accounting for EUR 6.7m received for the sale
of the Aachen office building and the payment of a EUR 8.2m dividend to </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRONs</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> shareholders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trade receivables</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> decreased from </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 38.8m</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">as of December&nbsp;31, 2008 to EUR 26.0m as of
June&nbsp;30, 2009 in line with the
changed business volume.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.
Opportunities and Risks</font></b><a name="a5_OpportunitiesAndRisks_043439"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON believes that the following market trends and <b>opportunities</b> of the relevant end user markets could have a
positive effect on future business:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Short
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Continuing increase of
capacity for the production of LED backlighting for LCD-Screens (liquid crystal
displays)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further increased adoption of
LEDs in automotive (e.g. interior lighting, headlights and rear lights).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mid
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Early street light orders
encouraged by government support and incentive programs for energy efficient
and environmentally friendly lighting applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further development progress
leading to a broader application of LEDs in general/interior lighting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pioneering e-paper applications
being trialed by newspapers and e-retailers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased emergence of high
volume Silicon Carbide (SiC) production applications and emerging hybrid
automotive and photovoltaic transistor applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of plastic
electronics / flexible organic TFT backplanes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of next generation
NAND and DRAM memory applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased development activity
for specialized compound solar cell applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Long
Term</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Progress in research
activities leading to technologies for OLED lighting and organic material large
area deposition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Intensified activity in the
development of new complex semiconductor material applications as substituting
materials in the silicon semiconductor industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of new
applications using Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Carbon
Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is exposed to a series of <b>risks</b>
which are described in detail in chapter 7. &#147;Risk Report&#148; of the Annual Report
2008 and in the section &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in AIXTRON&#146;s 2008 20-F-Report, which has
been filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission on March&nbsp;12,
2009. Copies of the Company&#146;s most recent Annual Report and Form&nbsp;20-F are
available on the Company&#146;s website at http://www.aixtron.com (sections &#147;Investors/Reports&#148;
and &#147;Investors/US-Listing&#148;), as well as on the SEC&#146;s website at
http://www.sec.gov.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April&nbsp;7,
2009, the district court in Aachen judged in AIXTRON&#146;s favor in the German
action for a negative declaratory judgment against International Rectifier
Corporation (&#147;I.R.&#148;) and the German counterclaim of I.R. was dismissed, the
judgement is final. In February&nbsp;2009, the United States District Court in
California dismissed I.R.&#146;s federal claims against AIXTRON. I.R. subsequently
dropped its federal claims and re-filed its California state law claims in the
California Superior Court for Los Angeles County. AIXTRON continues to reject
all allegations involved and continues to defend itself against the allegations
and claims raised in the action.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first half of 2009, AIXTRON Management was
not aware of any further significant additions or changes in the risks as
described in the 2008 Annual Report/20-F-Report referred to above.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">6. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Outlook</font><a name="a6_Outlook_043444"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With order activity
picking up again in Q2/2009 (an increase of 85% over Q1/2009), in line with our
previous predictions, we are becoming more positive on the continuation of the
LED investment cycle.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We remain confident in
our business model and continue to be optimistic about the increasingly evident
medium to long-term trends towards the increasing penetration of LED
technologies in a wide range of applications and the consequent positive effect
on future order intake.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
enter the third quarter of the year with a much more positive customer
sentiment in comparison to the prior quarter. We have seen increasing momentum
of LED technology demand, a rapid return to very high customer production
utilization rates, and an improved visibility of LED manufacturers&#146; demand
requirements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The combination of
these positive developments enables us to increase our guidance for fiscal year
2009: We believe that in 2009, AIXTRON can deliver revenues in the range of EUR
230-250m with an EBIT margin in the range of 12-13%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Management will continue to closely watch the
volatility of the USD/EUR exchange rate and the potential effects on the
company&#146;s revenues and profitability.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the second half of the year, the Company plans
to continue to invest in laboratory equipment and the further implementation of
the group-wide SAP Enterprise Software System.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company continues to have sufficient funds to be
able to support the planned business activities in the foreseeable future.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at June 30, 2009, AIXTRON had no binding agreements
for participation financing, company acquisition or transfers of parts of the
Company.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Consolidated Balance Sheet</font><a name="a2_ConsolidatedBalanceSheet_043546"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="55%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:55.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 10.0pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">in EUR thousands</font></b></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Additional Disclosures<a name="AdditionalDisclosures_043601"></a></font></b></h1>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Accounting Policies</font><a name="a1_AccountingPolicies_043602"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This consolidated interim financial report of AIXTRON
AG has been prepared in accordance with International Financial Reporting
Standards (IFRS) applicable for Interim Financial Reporting, IAS 34.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It was not audited according to &#167; 317 HGB or reviewed
by a certified auditor.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accounting policies adopted in this interim
financial report are consistent with those followed in the preparation of the
Group&#146;s annual financial statements for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
consolidated interim financial statements of AIXTRON AG include the following
operating subsidiaries (collectively referred to as &#147;AIXTRON&#148;, &#147;the AIXTRON
Group&#148;, or &#147;the Company&#148;): AIXTRON,&nbsp;Inc., Sunnyvale, California (USA);
AIXTRON Ltd., Cambridge (United Kingdom); AIXTRON AB, Lund (Sweden); AIXTRON
Korea Co. Ltd., Seoul (South Korea); AIXTRON KK, Tokyo (Japan); and AIXTRON
Taiwan Co. Ltd., Hsinchu-City (Taiwan). There were no significant changes in
the consolidated group of companies in comparison with December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Segment Reporting</font><a name="a2_SegmentReporting_043605"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following
segment information has been prepared in accordance with IFRS 8 &#147;Operating
Segments&#148;. As AIXTRON has only one Operating Segment, the information provided
relates only to geographical data.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and sells its products in Asia,
Europe, and the United States, mainly through its direct sales organization and
cooperation partners.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In presenting information on the basis of geographical
segments, segment revenue is based on the geographical location of customers.
Segment assets are based on the geographical location of the assets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As part of the Genus Inc. acquisition transaction,
which was completed in March&nbsp;2005, a trust for the employee stock options
of the Genus employees was set up, into which an appropriate number of AIXTRON
ADSs were deposited.</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.
Employees</font></b><a name="a4_Employees_043611"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total number of employees, including members of
the Executive Board and apprentices, rose from 616 on June&nbsp;30, 2008 to 622
persons on June&nbsp;30, 2009.</font></p>
