<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*) including Executive Board
and apprentices</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">5. Management</font></b><a name="a5_Management_043615"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
compared to December&nbsp;31, 2008, there were no changes to the composition of
the Company&#146;s Executive and Supervisory Boards as of June&nbsp;30, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">6. Related Party Transactions</font></b><a name="a6_RelatedPartyTransactions_043617"></a></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
did not conclude or carry out any material transactions with related parties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">7.
Post-Balance Sheet Date Events</font></b><a name="a7_PostbalanceSheetDateEvents_043618"></a></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There
were no business events with a potentially significant effect on AIXTRON&#146;s
results of operation, financial position or net assets after June&nbsp;30,
2009, of which the Management is aware.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Responsibility Statement<a name="ResponsibilityStatement_044126"></a></font></b></h1>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 6.5pt .0001pt 0in;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the best of our
knowledge, and in accordance with the applicable reporting principles for
interim financial reporting, the interim consolidated financial statements for
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2009 give a true and fair view of the
assets, liabilities, financial position and profit or loss of the group, and
the interim management report of the group includes a fair review of the
development and performance of the business and the position of the group,
together with a description of the principal </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">opportunities
and risks associated with the expected development of the group for the
remaining months of the financial year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Herzogenrath, July&nbsp;2009</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
Aktiengesellschaft, Herzogenrath</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Executive Board</font></p>
